### Phase J — Intent & Selection Quality

Highest-impact work. The core value of AIC is picking the right files — if selection is wrong, nothing else matters. Language providers also ensure the summarisation ladder produces semantically safe output per language (correct indentation, signatures, symbol extraction).

| Component                        | Status | Package              | Description                                                      |
| -------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Richer intent keyword extraction | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Expanded keywords: migrate, debug, changelog, e2e, fixture, etc. |
| Intent-aware file discovery      | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Pre-filters repo by keyword and include/exclude patterns         |
| Import graph signal (TS/JS)      | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | BFS over import graph; score by dependency distance              |
| GenericImportProvider (Py/Go/Rs) | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Regex imports for .py/.go/.rs/.java before AST providers         |
| PythonProvider (AST-safe)        | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | tree-sitter: imports, signatures, docstrings, symbols            |
| GoProvider                       | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | tree-sitter: imports, functions, methods, types                  |
| RustProvider                     | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | tree-sitter: use, functions, structs, impls                      |
| JavaProvider                     | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | tree-sitter: imports, methods, classes, interfaces               |
| RubyProvider                     | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Regex: require/load, def/class/module                            |
| PhpProvider                      | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Regex: require/include/use, function/class                       |
| CssProvider                      | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Regex: @import, selector-like lines                              |

### Phase L — Transformers & Guard

Incremental output quality improvements, measured by Phase K benchmarks. New transformers must be semantically safe — never break indentation (Python/YAML/Makefile), JSX syntax, or templating languages. Each transformer needs file-type safety tests.

| Component                                   | Status | Package               | Description                                                                                                                      |
| ------------------------------------------- | ------ | --------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| LicenseHeaderStripper                       | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Strips leading license/copyright/SPDX comment blocks                                                                             |
| Base64InlineDataStripper                    | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Replaces data:base64 URLs with placeholder                                                                                       |
| LongStringLiteralTruncator                  | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Truncates string literals >200 chars                                                                                             |
| DocstringTrimmer                            | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Trims long Python/JSDoc docstrings                                                                                               |
| CssVariableSummarizer                       | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Keeps :root; replaces other rule bodies with "[N declarations]"                                                                  |
| TypeDeclarationCompactor                    | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Collapses .d.ts type/interface/enum to single line                                                                               |
| TestStructureExtractor                      | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Strips describe/it/test bodies; keeps names and structure                                                                        |
| ImportDeduplicator                          | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Merges duplicate imports per file                                                                                                |
| HtmlToMarkdownTransformer                   | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Converts HTML to Markdown; strips script/style                                                                                   |
| SvgDescriber                                | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Replaces SVG with "[SVG: viewBox, N elements, bytes]"                                                                            |
| YamlCompactor                               | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Strips YAML comments; normalises indent; collapses single-key blocks                                                             |
| MinifiedCodeSkipper                         | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Placeholder for .min.js/.min.css, dist/, build/                                                                                  |
| AutoGeneratedSkipper                        | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Placeholder when header contains "auto-generated"/"code generated"                                                               |
| EnvExampleRedactor                          | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Redacts KEY=value to KEY= in .env.example/.env.sample/.env.template (secret protection)                                          |
| SchemaFileCompactor                         | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Compacts JSON Schema, GraphQL, Prisma, Proto                                                                                     |
| Transformer safety tests                    | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/  | Safety tests (indentation, YAML, JSX preserved)                                                                                  |

| show aic status with time range                          | Done   | shared + mcp  | Rolling N-day window (1..STATUS_TIME_RANGE_DAYS_MAX): MCP `aic_status` `timeRangeDays`, CLI `npx @jatbas/aic status <N>d`, human table **Time range** row; `StatusSummaryFilter` / `notBeforeInclusive` on all relevant `compilation_log` aggregates including distinct-project gate and breakdown (Task 255) |

### Phase M 0.5 — MCP-only (Drop CLI)

CLI package removed. User questions ("Is it working?", "What just happened?", "How much has it saved me?") are answered via MCP resources and prompt commands inside the editor.

| Component                                                           | Status | Delivered as                                                                               | Description                                                                      |
| ------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |

| Redesign `aic status`                                               | Done   | aic_status tool with `budgetMaxTokens`, `budgetUtilizationPct` + "show aic status"         | Project stats + budget utilisation                                               |
| Remove `aic compile` / `inspect` / `report`                         | Done   | CLI package removed; MCP tools `aic_compile`, `aic_inspect` are the interface              | MCP-only; no CLI package                                                         |
| `aic init`                                                          | Done   | `npx @aic/mcp init` + auto-init on MCP startup (`ensureAicDir`)                            | One-time or auto project setup                                                   |

| Shell diagnostics (`status` / `last` / `chat-summary` / `projects`) | Done   | `npx @jatbas/aic` subcommands, read-only global DB, shared payload builders with MCP tools | Fast terminal parity with aic_status / aic_last / chat aggregates / aic_projects |

## Phase 1.0 — OSS Release (completed phases)

### Phase N — Specification Compiler

Compile project specifications and documentation into structured context alongside code. Rules, ADRs, and design docs are selected and compressed through the same pipeline, ensuring the model has both code and spec awareness.

| Component                          | Status | Package              | Description                                                                 |
| ---------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Spec file discovery and scoring    | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Discovers and scores project ADRs, rules, and design docs alongside code    |
| Spec-aware summarisation tier      | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Heading-based tier compression for .md/.mdc spec files                      |
| Spec injection in prompt assembler | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Injects a ## Specification section with project rules and ADRs into context |

### Phase O — Agentic Session Tracking

Session-level intelligence for multi-step agent workflows. Deduplication prevents re-compiling identical context across turns; completed steps are formatted into a deterministic session context header (not model summarisation); Step 3 clamps the context budget when session-derived or wire `conversationTokens` is present (fixed 128k/4k/500 math in `BudgetAllocator` — not utilization learning or formula-derived bases).

| Component                                    | Status | Package              | Deps                | Description                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| -------------------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------- | ------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Session-level compilation deduplication      | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                   | Avoids re-sending files already shown in the current agent session                                                                                                                                    |
| Conversation context compression             | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Session-level dedup | Formats prior conversation steps as a deterministic numbered list injected as session context header                                                                                                  |
| Adaptive budget allocation (session history) | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Session-level dedup | Clamps Step 3 budget via `min(base, f(conversationTokens))` using fixed literals in `budget-allocator.ts` when tokens are wired or summed from session steps — not auto-tuning from `compilation_log` |
| Session tracking storage (migration)         | Done   | shared/src/storage/  | —                   | Persistent session state across turns (migration + store)                                                                                                                                             |

### Phase P — Context Quality, Token Efficiency & Compilation Performance

Context quality and compilation performance beyond the base heuristic pipeline. Selection and context shaping include symbol-level intent matching (ContextBench 2026), bidirectional import graph scoring with reverse dependency walking (InlineCoder/RIG 2026 — 12.2% accuracy gain), adaptive scoring weights per task class, a RIG-style structural context map (57.8% efficiency gain), and chunk-level file inclusion that surfaces relevant functions or blocks instead of always sending whole files. Throughput adds granular per-file transformation caching, scan-path improvements (`fast-glob` `stats: true` to avoid a second full-tree `fs.statSync` pass, async scanning instead of synchronous glob plus per-file stat), and a watched in-memory RepoMap so subsequent `getRepoMap()` returns without rescanning. All implemented within AIC's hexagonal architecture via new classes/interfaces (OCP).

| Component                                       | Status | Package              | Deps                     | Description                                                                                                                             |
| ----------------------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------- | ------------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Adaptive scoring weights per task class         | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                        | Per-task-class weight profiles (bugfix → recency, refactor → import proximity)                                                          |
| Reverse dependency walking (bidirectional BFS)  | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                        | Invert import graph to also score files that import seed files                                                                          |
| Symbol-level intent matching                    | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                        | Match intent subject tokens against exported symbol names via subjectTokens                                                             |
| Structural context map (RIG-inspired)           | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                        | Compact project architecture summary injected before code context                                                                       |
| Chunk-level file inclusion                      | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Symbol-level intent (#1) | Include only relevant functions/blocks instead of whole files                                                                           |
| Granular file-level transformation cache        | Done   | shared/src/storage/  | —                        | Per-file L0–L3 output cached by content hash; skip unchanged files on recompile                                                         |
| Scan: eliminate double-stat via fast-glob stats | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | —                        | Use fast-glob `stats: true` to avoid second `fs.statSync` pass over all files                                                           |
| Scan: async file system I/O                     | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Eliminate double-stat    | Async `fast-glob` via `GlobProvider.findWithStats` (`stats: true`); no `fg.sync` or second full-tree stat pass over all files           |
| Scan: cached RepoMap with file watcher          | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | Async file system I/O    | `WatchingRepoMapSupplier`: in-memory map per root, recursive `fs.watch`, cache hit skips inner scan; per-path stat on watch events only |

### Phase Q — Research-Backed Quality & Security

Research-driven improvements to context retrieval quality, token efficiency, security, and prompt assembly. Motivated by: ContextBench (2026) for process-level evaluation at file/block/line granularity; SWE-Pruner (Jan 2026) for task-aware line-level pruning (23–54% additional token reduction); InlineCoder (Jan 2026) for confidence estimation via deterministic proxies; "Lost in the Middle" (2023–2026) for prompt assembly ordering; and emerging prompt injection analysis targeting coding assistant tool execution. Builds on Phase P foundations (chunk-level inclusion, symbol matching, import graph). Editor-side compilation enforcement (hooks, pre-tool-use gating, trigger rule) is documented in `documentation/project-plan.md` §2.2.1; a middleware-style enforcer in the model call path remains deferred beyond the current integration layer.

| Component                                              | Status | Package              | Deps             | Description                                                                              |
| ------------------------------------------------------ | ------ | -------------------- | ---------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Constraints preamble in prompt assembler (LitM)        | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                | Duplicate top-3 constraints as short preamble before bulk context to mitigate LitM       |
| `contextCompleteness` confidence signal in CompileMeta | Done   | shared/src/core/     | —                | Unresolved imports, missing symbols, intent token coverage in CompilationMeta            |
| Line-level pruner within matched chunks (SWE-Pruner)   | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | Chunk-level (#P) | Score lines within L0 chunks against intent tokens; remove irrelevant, keep syntax       |
| `CommandInjectionScanner` (GuardScanner)               | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                | Detect `$(...)`, backtick substitution, pipe chains in comments/docs                     |
| `MarkdownInstructionScanner` (GuardScanner)            | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —                | Detect high-risk instruction payloads in markdown/doc files                              |
| Block/line-level gold annotations in benchmark suite   | Done   | test/benchmarks/     | —                | Enrich gold set from path-only to block/line ranges per file for ContextBench-style eval |
| Per-task-class precision/recall metrics in benchmarks  | Done   | test/benchmarks/     | Gold annotations | Precision/recall at file, block, line granularity grouped by task class                  |

### Phase R — MCP Server Security Hardening

Industry-standard security hardening for the AIC MCP server, motivated by the official MCP Security Best Practices spec, the Cloud Security Alliance MCP Server Top 10, and a code-level gap analysis. Addresses six confirmed gaps: `projectRoot`/`configPath` path traversal, unconstrained `intent`/`conversationId` character sets, missing compilation timeout enforcement, absent tool-invocation audit log, and `compiledPrompt` exposure in the aic_last response (now aic_last tool). All changes are bounded to `mcp/src/` and `shared/src/storage/migrations/` — zero pipeline or core changes.

| Component                                            | Status | Package                               | Deps | Description                                                                                                              |
| ---------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ------------------------------------- | ---- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| Schema hardening: path containment + char-set guards | Done   | mcp/src/schemas/ + mcp/src/handlers/  | —    | `projectRoot`/`configPath` path-traversal guard; `intent` control-char strip; `conversationId`/`modelId` allow-lists     |
| Compilation timeout enforcement                      | Done   | mcp/src/handlers/                     | —    | `Promise.race` with 30s `TimeoutError` wrapping `runner.run(request)` in compile-handler                                 |
| Tool-invocation audit log (migration + store write)  | Done   | shared/src/storage/migrations/ + mcp/ | —    | New `tool_invocation_log` migration and append-on-call write from compose root                                           |
| aic_last compiledPrompt removal                      | Done   | mcp/src/server.ts                     | —    | Strip raw `compiledPrompt` from aic_last tool response; return token count and guard status only                         |
| aic_inspect response cap (strip resolvedContent)     | Done   | mcp/src/handlers/                     | —    | Map `trace.selectedFiles` before `JSON.stringify`; omit `resolvedContent` so inspect responses cannot self-flood context |
| `security.md` MCP Top 10 coverage table              | Done   | documentation/                        | —    | Explicit mapping of AIC vs MCP Server Top 10 risks; documents what is covered, deferred, or N/A                          |

### Phase S — Cursor Hook Upgrades

Cursor exposes hooks AIC was not yet using: sessionEnd, preCompact (observational only), subagentStart (gating only — no context injection), postToolUse (with `additional_context`), stop (with `followup_message`). This phase aligns existing hooks to the official schema, adds new lifecycle hooks (sessionEnd, stop quality check, afterFileEdit tracking), improves session-scoped env propagation, and updates documentation to reflect the corrected Cursor capability picture.

| stop quality check + afterFileEdit tracker (Task 111) | Done   | .cursor/hooks/ + mcp/                       | —        | Track edited files; run lint/typecheck on stop; auto-fix via `followup_message`                                                        |

### Phase W — Global Server & Per-Project Isolation

One global MCP server in `~/.cursor/mcp.json`; one DB at `~/.aic/aic.sqlite`. Each `aic_compile` supplies `projectRoot`; server uses a `ScopeRegistry` for per-project scopes. Stable UUIDv7 in `.aic/project-id` per project; duplicate config triggers a warning. See `implementation-spec.md` §Phase W for full details.

| Component                                       | Status | Package                                      | Deps          | Description                                                                                      |
| ----------------------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------------------------------- | ------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| W01: Cross-platform path normalisation          | Done   | shared/src/core/ + adapters/                 | —             | normaliseProjectRoot() in paths.ts; absolute, strip trailing slash, Windows drive lowercased     |
| W02: Schema migration 011 (columns only)        | Done   | shared/src/storage/migrations/               | W01           | project_root column + projects table; migration 011                                              |
| W03: Stable project ID                          | Done   | shared/src/storage/ + mcp/src/               | W02           | UUIDv7 in .aic/project-id; ensureProjectInit; reconcile renames in projects + per-project tables |
| W04: Store constructor projectRoot param        | Done   | shared/src/storage/ + mcp/src/               | W01           | All 9 per-project stores take projectRoot: AbsolutePath; createProjectScope + server pass it     |
| W05: Store SQL project_root queries             | Done   | shared/src/storage/                          | W02, W04      | All INSERT/SELECT/UPDATE/DELETE in 9 stores use WHERE project_root = ?                           |
| W06: ScopeRegistry class                        | Done   | shared/src/storage/                          | W01           | getOrCreate(projectRoot), close(); Map keyed by normalised path                                  |
| W07: Wire ScopeRegistry into server             | Done   | mcp/src/                                     | W03, W05, W06 | createMcpServer uses ScopeRegistry; compile handler gets scope per args.projectRoot              |

| W17: Merge all migrations into just one         | Done   | shared/src/storage/migrations/               | W16           | Single 001-initial-schema.ts; drop 14 incremental migrations                                     |
| W11: Per-folder disable                         | Done   | mcp/src/handlers/ + shared/src/config/       | W07           | aic.config.json "enabled": false → compile no-op, status shows Disabled                          |
| W12: Commands scoped by project                 | Done   | mcp/src/                                     | W07           | aic_status global + per-project; aic_last by conversation; aic_projects tool                     |
| Task 145: aic_status and aic_last MCP tools     | Done   | mcp/src/ + .cursor/rules/                    | W12           | aic_status/aic_last as MCP tools; prompt commands call tools                                     |
| W13: Documentation update                       | Done   | documentation/                               | W07, W16      | impl-spec, project-plan, security, AIC-architect: global DB + project_id                         |
| W14: Release 0.7.0                              | Done   | all                                          | W01-W13       | Version 0.7.0; changelog; tag, push, CI, GitHub release                                          |

---

## Phase 1.5 — Optimizations, Hardening & Simplification

Runtime CPU/memory/I/O optimizations, bootstrap reliability, cache file security hardening, model ID resolution simplification, cache pipeline audit and refactoring (prompt log, session markers, edited-files temp cache), integration shared utility extraction, and Claude hooks/plugin deduplication. Through sub-phase AO, tranches were bounded to `mcp/src/`, `shared/src/`, and `integrations/` (plus targeted `documentation/` for AO) with no broad pipeline algorithm refactors beyond per-phase notes. Phases X through AO are complete. **AP** is documentation and skill-path hygiene (progress narrative, `aic-progress.md` references, typo, budget prose vs `BudgetAllocator`). **AQ** extends `shared/src/pipeline/` selection using structured `toolOutputs.relatedFiles` and aligns compilation cache keys when that signal affects ranking. **AR** is maintainer quick fixes (executor verify skill table row 19, sanitized `listRoots`/bootstrap observability in `mcp/src/server.ts`). **AS** is the MCP `aic_compile_spec` foundation slice (Zod schema, stub/minimal handler, registration, tests, docs) — distinct from Phase N Done spec-**file** pipeline; inner `SpecificationCompiler` tier loop is out of scope for AS. **AV** tightens import-graph construction, removes dead `StatusRunner` surface, and aligns heuristic weights documentation with five-field `ScoringWeights`. **AW** delivers the deferred `SpecificationCompiler` vertical slice for `aic_compile_spec` (tier loop and handler integration; cross-call spec-cache and full `ContentTransformerPipeline` / `SummarisationLadder` reuse on file-backed inputs deferred to follow-on work). **AX** continues §2.7 with a verbatim-tier transformer and ladder integration slice and an async-capable `SpecificationCompiler` port; persistent cross-call SQLite cache for `aic_compile_spec` stays deferred until usage justifies it. **AY** closes import-graph integrity gaps (per-edge reverse-list allocation vs AV01 intent, read/parse failures via `ImportGraphFailureSink` in `buildEdges`) plus remaining `implementation-spec.md` import-graph semantics. **AZ** adds SQLite-backed read-through cache for `aic_compile_spec` per `documentation/project-plan.md` §2.7 Phase 1 roadmap. **BA** extends `SpecificationCompilerImpl` with `ContentTransformerPipeline` / `SummarisationLadder` on signature-path tier bodies beyond the shipped verbatim-only pre-pass. **BC** aligns the progress file header narrative with authoritative Done tables. **BB** closes the `documentation/project-plan.md` §2.7 Phase 1 remainder: main-pipeline transform and ladder on `spec.codeBlocks`, `spec.prose`, and demoted type bodies in `SpecificationCompilerImpl`, with documentation updates in `implementation-spec.md` and `project-plan.md` §2.7. **BD** post-BB hygiene: progress header reconciliation (BD01); cache-hit narrative vs `compile-handler.ts` / `compilation-runner.ts` in `project-plan.md` / `implementation-spec.md` (BD02 Done); weak-intent `compilation_log` lookup plan fix (BD03, `get-last-intent-for-conversation.ts`). **BE** ships read-only rolling utilisation from `compilation_log` via a core port and SQLite adapter; allocator feedback stays deferred until KPI work (`documentation/tasks/progress/aic-progress.md:781`, `documentation/project-plan.md:776`).

### Phase AT — Hot-Path Performance Patches

Correctness and allocation improvements in three pipeline steps and the file content reader. None change observable behavior; all reduce GC pressure or SQL round-trips.

| Component                                     | Status | Package              | Deps | Description                                                                                                                                    |
| --------------------------------------------- | ------ | -------------------- | ---- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| AT01: Line-Level Pruner Accumulator Fix       | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —    | Replace `reduce`+spread accumulator in `computeKeepSet` with `flatMap` to eliminate O(n²) allocations per matched line                         |
| AT02: Summarisation Ladder Single-Pass        | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ | —    | Min-heap of row indices keyed by `compareDemotionPriority` replaces per-step `findLowestIdx` scan; O(log n) per demotion step, same tie-breaks |
| AT03: Purge Expired Single-Query Optimization | Done   | shared/src/storage/  | —    | Combine three sequential queries in `purgeExpired` into one transaction and eliminate the third full-table rescan                              |
| AT04: LRU Cache Eviction Optimization         | Done   | shared/src/adapters/ | —    | Verify and document the hit-promotion Map.delete+set pattern in `CachingFileContentReader`; confirm O(1) eviction semantics                    |

### Phase AU — Compilation Transparency

AIC selects and compresses files deterministically, but users currently cannot see _why_ a file was chosen or dropped — only that it was. This phase surfaces per-file heuristic scores and exclusion reasons in `aic_last` output, giving developers the forensic data they need to diagnose selection misses and tune rule packs. It also declares a structured output schema on `aic_compile` so downstream tooling can consume compilation results programmatically without text-parsing the response string.

| Component                                                        | Status | Package           | Deps       | Skill                      | Description                                                                                                                                           |
| ---------------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ----------------- | ---------- | -------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| AU01: Compilation Selection Trace                                | Done   | mcp/src/handlers/ | —          | `aic-task-planner`         | Extend `aic_last` response with `selectedFilesWithScores` (path + score + signals) and `excludedFilesWithReasons` (path + score + reason)             |
| AU02: MCP Output Schema Declaration                              | Done   | mcp/src/schemas/  | AU01       | `aic-task-planner`         | After SDK spike confirms `outputSchema` support in `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk@1.29.0`, declare output schemas on `aic_compile` and `aic_compile_spec` |
| AU03: implementation-spec.md Update for Compilation Transparency | Done   | documentation/    | AU01, AU02 | `aic-documentation-writer` | Document new `aic_last` selection trace fields and `outputSchema` declaration on `aic_compile`                                                        |
| AU04: README.md Update for Compilation Transparency              | Done   | documentation/    | AU01       | `aic-documentation-writer` | Expand the "No visibility" row in "What it helps with" to describe per-file score visibility in `show aic last`                                       |
| AU05: Cross-envelope conversation ID and hook runtime guards     | Done   | integrations/     | 296        | `aic-task-executor`        | `conversation_id` fallbacks in `conversation-id.cjs`, explicit `editorId` in Claude hooks, `cursor_version` guards on Claude and Cursor hook scripts  |

### Phase BF — Near-budget selection discipline

Structural fix for the selection failure mode surfaced by the 2026-04-22 near-ceiling selection-trace audit: `compilation_log` N=9,182 over 53 days; 7 rows (0.076%) exceeded 115,200 tokens (90% of 128k); 100% were `task_class=general` + `trigger_source=tool_gate`; 6/7 were dominated by `.git/` plumbing (e.g. `e0a79ce2…` selected 15 files of which all 15 start with `.git/`) ranked purely on `recency × sizePenalty` with every semantic signal (`pathRelevance`, `importProximity`, `symbolRelevance`, `ruleBoostCount`) at zero. Symptom has been unobserved since 2026-04-19 without a targeted code change; underlying `HeuristicSelector` has no minimum-relevance floor (`shared/src/pipeline/heuristic-selector.ts:164-179` — score is a plain weighted sum admitted to `fitToBudgetWithTrace` whenever > 0) and `DEFAULT_NEGATIVE_PATTERNS` root-anchors `!.git/**` without covering nested `.git/` directories (`shared/src/adapters/default-ignore-patterns.ts:6`). This phase makes the defense structural, not coincidental.

Success metric for the phase: **zero future rows with `tokens_compiled ≥ 115,200` that contain any `.git/**`-prefixed path in `selection_trace_json.selectedFiles`**, measured over rolling 30-day window on `~/.aic/aic.sqlite`.

| Component                                                       | Status | Package                                                 | Deps | Skill               | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| --------------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ------------------------------------------------------- | ---- | ------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| BF01: Repomap `.git/` regression test                           | Done   | shared/src/adapters/**tests**/                          | —    | `aic-task-executor` | Shipped in `341-bf01-repomap-git-regression-test.md`: Vitest `file_system_repo_map_supplier_never_returns_dot_git_paths` in `shared/src/adapters/__tests__/file-system-repo-map-supplier.test.ts` with real `FastGlobAdapter` + `IgnoreAdapter`; fixture `.git/{HEAD,FETCH_HEAD,refs/heads/main,objects/ab/cdefghijklmnop,worktrees/x/HEAD}` plus `src/visible.ts`; asserts no `.git/` or nested `/.git/` paths and visible file remains listed. No production code change.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| BF02: HeuristicSelector zero-semantic-signal floor              | Done   | shared/src/pipeline/ + `shared/src/core/types/`         | —    | `aic-task-executor` | Shipped in `342-bf02-heuristic-selector-zero-semantic-signal-floor.md`: `EXCLUSION_REASON.ZERO_SEMANTIC_SIGNAL`; `partitionZeroSemanticSignal` before `eligible.toSorted`; trace order `[...rule, ...zeroSemantic, ...budget]`; Zod literal; `heuristic_selector_rejects_zero_semantic_signal_candidates`; temporary integration `defaultRulePack` `src/**` boost until BF06 (`343-bf06-glob-match-nested-suffix-star.md`) restored `**/*.ts`; `test/benchmarks/expected-selection/1.json` narrowed to TS paths under the new floor.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

Verified on main: `pnpm lint`, `pnpm typecheck`, `pnpm test` (988 passed, 1 skipped), `pnpm knip`, `pnpm lint:clones`.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |

Pure adapter change; no pipeline impact.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| BF05: Near-ceiling soft diagnostic in `show aic last`           | Done   | mcp/src/                                                | BE03 | `aic-task-executor` | Shipped ad-hoc (no task file): `mcp/src/diagnostic-payloads.ts` `buildLastPayload` adds `budgetUtilizationPct`; `mcp/src/format-diagnostic-output.ts` `formatLastTable` appends footnote line when utilization ≥90 (percent scale; `resolveBudgetUtilizationPercent` 0–100): `⚠ budget utilisation ≥ 90% — review `aic_last` selection trace or tighten intent` (`aic_last` is an MCP tool, not a CLI flag). Purely read-only formatting; no new SQL, no allocator writes. Vitest `format_last_flags_near_ceiling_budget_utilisation` covers the ≥90% branch, the <90% branch, and the null-utilisation cache-hit zero-file branch. **Note:** threshold is conservatively early until BH01 ships — the 2026-04-23 audit (`.aic/runs/diagnostic-numbers-audit-2026-04-23/findings.md` FAIL #1) shows `budgetUtilizationPct` over-reports by ~1.7pp on opus-class models because four display sites divide `tokensCompiled` by the hardcoded `128_000 − 4_000 − 500 = 123_500` default instead of the allocator's model-derived `totalBudget` (e.g. `125_500` for `claude-opus-4-7`). BF05 is mechanically independent of BH01 (read-only formatting over a computed field) and its warning behavior is conservative (over-warns, never misses), so BF05 can ship ahead of BH01; the meter becomes honest once BH01 lands. **Success:** at least one golden fixture includes the line and fenced stdout discipline (`aic-architect.mdc` §Prompt Commands) still passes. |

### Phase BG — Large-context attention and prose-density mitigations

Structural completion of the two remaining actionable items from `documentation/research/2026-04-09-large-context-token-waste-mitigation.md` after 2026-04-22 verification that Recommendations #1 (model-aware budget with 0.65 effective factor via `MODEL_CONTEXT_WINDOWS` in `shared/src/data/model-context-windows.ts` and `resolveModelDerivedContextWindow` in `shared/src/pipeline/compilation-runner.ts:323-336`), #2 (budget-scaled max-files in `resolveAutoMaxFiles` at `shared/src/core/run-pipeline-steps.ts:142-151`, cap `MAX_FILES_UPPER_BOUND = 300`), and #4 (conversation-id injection in `integrations/claude/hooks/aic-inject-conversation-id.cjs` and `integrations/cursor/hooks/AIC-inject-conversation-id.cjs` activating `getPreviouslyShownFiles` at `shared/src/core/run-pipeline-steps.ts:267-286`) are already shipped. Recommendation #6 (budget headroom in `aic status`) is **not** added — it is already exposed as `budgetUtilizationPct` in `formatStatusTable` (`mcp/src/format-diagnostic-output.ts:317-319`) and will be reinforced by BF05. Two structural gaps remain at 1M effective-window models (`claude-opus-4.6`, `claude-sonnet-4.6`, `gemini-2.5-pro` at `shared/src/data/model-context-windows.ts:11-23`): (a) `PromptAssembler.assemble` (`shared/src/pipeline/prompt-assembler.ts:73-82`) renders files in a single front-loaded order so all relevance mass sits at the head, aggravating the "lost in the middle" attention profile (Liu et al., arxiv 2307.03172; Chroma 2025 "Context Rot" multi-model eval; NVIDIA RULER); and (b) the transformer pipeline has no prose-density pass for `.md`/`.mdx`/`.rst`/`.txt`, so markdown sections that ride the spec ladder (`specification-compiler.ts`) carry frontmatter, multi-blank-line padding, and long URLs into the compiled prompt at verbatim density.

Success metric for the phase: on a fixture compile with `sessionContext.contextWindow` derived via `resolveModelDerivedContextWindow("claude-opus-4.6")` and ≥20 selected files, (1) the highest-relevance file path appears at the first `### <path>` under `## Context` **and** as the sole entry under a trailing `## Context (reinforced)` block, with no other file duplicated; (2) a representative README-shaped markdown fixture's `transformedTokens` after `ContentTransformerPipeline.transform` is ≤ 0.85 × `originalTokens` with `transformersApplied` including `"prose-density"`.

### Phase BH — Diagnostic numbers audit remediation

Fix the 13 defects catalogued by the 2026-04-23 diagnostic-numbers audit (`.aic/runs/diagnostic-numbers-audit-2026-04-23/findings.md`) so every number surfaced by the five `show aic …` CLIs and their MCP equivalents (`aic_status`, `aic_last`, `aic_chat_summary`, `aic_quality_report`, `aic_projects`) matches its label and formula exactly. Root defect: `budgetUtilizationPct` is derived at four sites from a hardcoded `128_000 − 4_000 − 500 = 123_500` default denominator while `BudgetAllocator` uses the model-derived window (`resolveModelDerivedContextWindow(modelId) − RESERVED − TEMPLATE`, e.g. `200_000 × 0.65 − 4_000 − 500 = 125_500` for `claude-opus-4-7`), so every opus-class compile is over-reported by ~1.7pp on display; one of the four sites (`mcp/src/handlers/compile-handler.ts:280-286` `tryRecordQualitySnapshot`) persists the wrong value into `quality_snapshots.budget_utilisation` so historical rows cannot be retroactively corrected from the log (observed live on `ea80b718`: `budget_utilisation = 1.054` stored). Secondary defects span hero-line subject/object confusion on `aic last` (`"24 of 730 files forwarded (89.0% excluded)"` parses as files but is tokens), cache-hit `files_selected = 0` misrepresentation at `shared/src/pipeline/compilation-runner.ts:80`, label drift on `Avg context precision` (ratio-of-sums not average), `Guard scans (lifetime)` (time-filtered when windowed), `Context builds (today)` (UTC boundary), `Installation` (global, not project-scoped), `projects.last_seen_at` (drifts from actual last compile), ambiguous `N blocked` guard label (files, not findings), `.git/` paths still appearing in selection-trace top files pre-BF01, `Percentage` branded-type double semantics (ratio 0..1 in `CompilationMeta.tokenReductionPct` vs pct 0..100 in `StatusAggregates.avgReductionPct`), and silent model-ID normalization walk-down (`claude-opus-4-7` → `claude-opus-4` with no stderr warning).

Success metric for the phase: for any compilation with `modelId ∈ MODEL_CONTEXT_WINDOWS`, the displayed `budgetUtilizationPct` (in `aic_last`, `aic_status`, `aic_quality_report`) and the persisted `quality_snapshots.budget_utilisation` equal the allocator's actual `totalBudget` denominator to within floating-point tolerance of the value `BudgetAllocator.allocate` returned at compile time; all 13 label/scope defects listed in `findings.md` §Phase 5 are fixed or explicitly relabeled.

### Phase BI — Allocator / prompt-assembler drift

Close the real overshoot identified by the 2026-04-23 audit on compilation `ea80b718` (`tokens_compiled = 130_168 > totalBudget = 125_500` by 4_668 tokens, **3.72%** over allocator-granted budget) — independent of the Phase BH display bugs: even with the correct denominator the prompt exceeded the budget the allocator promised. Candidate root causes (`findings.md` §Phase 4): (a) `computeOverheadTokens` at `shared/src/core/run-pipeline-steps.ts:153-162` does not count per-file `### <path>` headers, code fences, `## Context` / `## Context (reinforced)` section headers, or separators injected by `PromptAssembler.assemble`; (b) spec-ladder `estimatedTokens` are pre-assembly estimates not re-counted post-render at `shared/src/core/run-pipeline-steps.ts:230-233`; (c) `SummarisationLadder.compress` knapsack permits last-file overshoot up to one tier delta; (d) `structuralMap` token count measured standalone at `shared/src/core/run-pipeline-steps.ts:213` may differ from its rendered form in the assembled prompt. This phase is **not** display work — it is pipeline instrumentation.

Success metric for the phase: on a synthetic fixture with 24 mid-size files at `sessionContext.contextWindow = resolveModelDerivedContextWindow("claude-opus-4-7")`, `tokenCounter.countTokens(assembledPrompt) ≤ totalBudget` in 100% of runs; on production data over the 30-day window after landing, zero `compilation_log` rows where `tokens_compiled > totalBudget` on non-cache compiles.
